PO'I NGO BOR GYUR PA'I SGOM LAM BAR CHAD MED LAM NAS, SA GNYIS
PA'I SKAD CIG THA MA'I BAR CHAD MED LAM GYIS BDEN 'DZIN LHAN
SKYES CHEN PO'I CHEN PO SPONG BAR BYED, SA GSUM PA THOB MA THAG
PA'I BAR CHAD MED LAM NAS SA GSUM PA'I SKAD CIG THA MA'I BAR
CHAD MED LAM GYIS BDEN 'DZIN LHAN SKYES CHEN

PO'I 'BRING GI SPONG GNYEN BYED PA NAS BZUNG STE RIM PA BZHIN
DU, SA BCU PA THOB MA THAG PA'I YE SHES NAS, SA BCU PA'I SKAD
CIG THA MA'I BAR CHAD MED LAM GYI BAR GYIS BDEN 'DZIN LHAN SKYES
CHUNG NGU CHUNG NGU'I SPONG GNYEN BYED DE, BDEN 'DZIN LHAN SKYES
CHUNG NGU'I CHUNG NGU LAS DNGOS SU GROL BA DANG

RNAM MKHYEN SKAD CIG DANG PO THOB PA DUS MNYAM PA'I PHYIR, NYAN
THOS KYI BAR CHAD MED LAM CHUNG 'BRING CHEN PO DGU RIM GYIS
SKYES STOBS KYIS GANG ZAG GI BDAG 'DZIN LHAN SKYES CHE 'BRING
CHUNG NGU DGU RIM GYIS SPONG BA'I DON YOD DE, NYAN THOS KYI
MTHONG LAM RNAM GROL LAM LAS LANGS RJES

SU BDAG 'DZIN LHAN SKYES SPONG BA'I PHYIR DU, GANG ZAG GI BDAG
MED LA RTZE GCIG TU MNYAM PAR GZHAG PA NAS SGOM LAM DU 'PHOS PA
YIN PA'I PHYIR, DER THAL, NYAN THOS KYI SGOM LAM BAR CHAD MED
LAM CHUNG 'BRING CHEN PO DGU RIM GYI SKYES STOBS KYIS BDAG 'DZIN
LHAN SKYES CHE

'BRING CHUNG NGU DGU RIM GYIS SPONG BAR BYED PA'I PHYIR, RANG
RGYAL GYI SGOM LAM BAR CHAD MED LAM GYIS GZUGS PHYI ROL DON
'DZIN GYI RTOGS PA LHAN SKYES DGU RIM GYIS SPONG PA'I DON YOD
DE, RANG RGYAL GYI MTHONG LAM RNAM GROL LAM LAS LANGS RJES SU
GZUGS PHYI ROL DON 'DZIN

GYI RTOG PA LHAN SKYES SPONG BA'I PHYIR DU GZUGS PHYI ROL DON
GYIS STONG BA LA RTZE GCIG TU MNYAM PAR GZHAG PA NAS SGOM LAM DU
'PHOS PA YIN PA'I PHYIR, DER THAL, RANG RGYAL GYI SGOM LAM BAR
CHAD MED LAM DGU SNGAR BZHIN RIM GYIS SKYES STOBS KYIS GZUGS
PHYIR ROL DON 'DZIN GYI

@53B RTOG PA LHAN SKYES CHE 'BRING CHUNG NGU DGU RIM GYIS SPONG
BA'I PHYIR, ,GSUM PA RTZOD PA SPONG BA LA, KHA CIG, THEG CHEN
GYI SGOM LAM BAR CHAD MED LAM CHUNG 'BRING CHEN PO DGU RIM GYIS
SKYES STOBS KYIS BDEN 'DZIN LHAN SKYES CHE 'BRING CHUNG NGU DGU
RIM GYIS SPONG BA DE MI 'THAD PAR THAL, BDEN 'DZIN

LHAN SKYES CHEN PO'I CHEN PO SPONG BA LA, THEG CHEN GYI SGOM LAM
BAR CHAD MED LAM CHEN PO'I CHEN PO RANG RGYUD LA BSKYED DGOS
PA'I PHYIR, DPER NA, DGRA STOBS LDAN 'DUL BA LA GSHED MA YANG
STOBS LDAN DGOS PA'I PHYIR ZER NA MA KHYAB, 'O NA, GOS LA CHAGS
PA'I DRI MA PHRA RAGS

GNYIS KYI NANG NAS RAGS PA SEL DKA' BA YIN PAR THAL, DGRA STOBS
LDAN 'DUL BA LA GSHED MA YANG STOBS LDAN DGOS PA'I PHYIR, STOBS
MTSUNGS SO, ,'DOD MI NUS TE, DE GNYIS KYI NANG NAS DRI MA RAGS
PA SEL SLA BA MNGON SUM GYIS GRUB PA'I PHYIR, KHA CIG,

PA BCU PA'I BAR CHAD MED LAM DE SA BCU PA'I SKAD CIG THA MA KHO
NAR SKYE BAR THAL, SA BCU PA'I NGOS SKAL GYI BDEN 'DZIN SPONG BA
LA BSOD NAMS KYI TSOGS RGYA CHEN POS ZIN DGOS PA'I PHYIR ZER NA
MA KHYAB, 'O NA, SA DGU PA MAN CHAD KYI BAR CHAD MED LAM DE YANG
DE'I THA MA KHO NAR

SKYE BAR THAL, SA DGU PA MAN CHAD KYI NGOS SKAL GYI SPANG BYA'I
BDEN 'DZIN SPONG BA LA BSOD NAMS KYIS TSOGS RGYA CHEN POS ZIN
DGOS PA GANG ZHIG ,SA BCU PA'I NGOS SKAL GYI BDEN 'DZIN LAS, SA
DGU PA MAN CHAD KYI NGOS SKAL GYI SPANG BYA SPONG SLA BA DE
BZHIN DU SA BCU PA'I NGOS SKAL

GYI SPANG BYA'I GNYEN PO LAS, SA DGU PA MAN CHAD KYI SPANG BYA'I
GNYEN PO STOBS CHUNG PA'I PHYIR, 'DOD NA 'GAL LO, ,KHA CIG ,SA
GSUM PA THOB MA THAG PA'I BAR CHAD MED LAM CHOS CAN, BDEN 'DZIN
LHAN SKYES CHEN PO'I 'BRING GI DNGOS GNYEN BAR CHAD MED LAM YIN
PAR THAL,

RANG GI NGOS SKAL GYI SPANG BYAR GYUR PA'I BDEN 'DZIN LHAN SKYES
CHEN PO'I 'BRING GI DNGOS GNYEN BAR CHAD MED LAM YIN PA'I PHYIR
ZER NA, 'O NA, NYAN THOS KYI MTHONG LAM BAR CHAD MED LAM CHOS
CAN, SGRIB PA'I DNGOS GNYEN BAR CHAD MED LAM YIN PAR THAL, RANG
GI NGOS SKAL GYI SGRIB PA'I DNGOS
